***digger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:digger.html>digger</a> (26729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dig</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.  In the sense of "Australian soldier" Attributed to the considerable time that <a href = vnd.unilang:soldiers.html>soldiers</a> spent digging trenches during World War I.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:digger.html>digger</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:diggers.html>diggers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A large piece of machinery that digs <a href = vnd.unilang:holes.html>holes</a> or trenches; an excavator.</li>
<li>A tool for digging.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  Sharon Bomgaars,  <cite>The <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>Best</a> Clubhouse Ever</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=uJfGh7Kof3MCamp;pg=PA143amp;dq=%22digger%22%7C%22diggers%22+-intitle:%22digger%7Cdiggers%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=Xrg8T4miN4fcmAXR6YW0Bwamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22digger%22%7C%22diggers%22%20-intitle%3A%22digger%7Cdiggers%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">[1]</a></sup>, page 143:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The post hole <b><a href = vnd.unilang:digger.html>digger</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> look ancient. I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> pretty certain myself that it hadn′t dug any <a href = vnd.unilang:holes.html>holes</a> for a long, long time.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A spade (playing card).</li>
<li>One who digs.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1997</b>,  Barbara J. <a href = vnd.unilang:wrede.html>Wrede</a>,  <cite>Civilizing Your Puppy</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=udex_pcxs8oCamp;pg=PA75amp;dq=%22digger%22%7C%22diggers%22+-intitle:%22digger%7Cdiggers%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=Xrg8T4miN4fcmAXR6YW0Bwamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22digger%22%7C%22diggers%22%20-intitle%3A%22digger%7Cdiggers%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">[2]</a></sup>, page 75:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">You′ve tried the supposedly sure method of squirting the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:digger.html>digger</a></b> with water from a hose, and that hasn′t worked.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>This step will discourage 99 percent of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:diggers.html>diggers</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2005</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gary.html>Gary</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. <dl><dd>Most <a href = vnd.unilang:retrievers.html>retrievers</a> are <i>not</i> inveterate <b><a href = vnd.unilang:diggers.html>diggers</a></b> — that′s a trait usually reserved for other breeds like wire-haired terriers and schnauzers.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A gold miner, one who digs for gold.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1853</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a> (editor),  <cite>Household <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>Words</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=rZRAAQAAIAAJamp;pg=PA64amp;dq=%22digger%22%7C%22diggers%22+-intitle:%22digger%7Cdiggers%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=HLw8T6fqAYrEmQWFy7XZBwamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22digger%22%7C%22diggers%22%20-intitle%3A%22digger%7Cdiggers%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">[3]</a></sup>, volume 21, page 64:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A successful Australian <a href = vnd.unilang:digger.html>digger</a> — successful, not merely in siftings and washings, but bearing the title, and its <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> credentials, of a “nuggetter” − <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> down from Forest Creek recently and <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> up his abode in a low lodging-house in Little Bourke Street, Melbourne.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dij.html>dij</a> (16138)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thio</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þeuhą</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tsjea</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thigh</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">þjó</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dij.html>dij</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dijen.html>dijen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dij.html>dijtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>thigh</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">do</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þiz</i>.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dik.html>dik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***dikt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dikt.html>dikt</a> (118440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href = vnd.unilang:dikt.html>dikt</a></i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> noun derived from <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dichten.html>dichten</a></i>, "to compose, authour (a poem)" (compare <a href = vnd.unilang:dikte.html>dikte</a>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:dikt.html>dikt</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>definite singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn">diktet</b>, <i>indefinite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:dikt.html>dikt</a></strong></b>, <i>definite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn">dikta</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">poem</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">literary piece written in verse</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><b>Diktet</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ei.html>ei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lita.html>lita</a> forteljing, <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> rommet <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> viktigare enn tidsforløpet.</i> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jan_Erik_Vold" class="extiw" title="w:Jan Erik Vold">Jan <a href = vnd.unilang:erik.html>Erik</a> Vold</a>)
<dl><dd><i>The poem <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a little story, but space <a href = vnd.unilang:matters.html>matters</a> more than lapse of time.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>fiction, pack of lies, invention (<i>compare <a href = vnd.unilang:dikte.html>dikte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opp.html>opp</a></i>)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> dette <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dikt.html>dikt</a></b> eller sannhet?</i>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> this fiction or truth?</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>(<i>poem</i>) <span class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:epos.html>epos</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nn">poem</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nn">poesi</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nn">rim</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nn">song</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:vers.html>vers</a></span></li>
<li>(<i>fiction</i>) <span class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:fabel.html>fabel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nn">fantasi</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:historie.html>historie</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nn">løgn</span>/<span class="Latn" lang="nn">lygn</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nn">diktar</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> (compare Dutch <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></i>)

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">close</span>
<dl><dd><i>Dei stod <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dikt.html>dikt</a></b> attmed kvarandre.</i>
<dl><dd><i>They stood close to each other.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>

***dill.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a> (31283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">dile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">dile</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a>, anise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">dilli</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dille.html>dille</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>Dill</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">dills</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>Anethum graveolens</i> (the type species of the genus <i>Anethum</i>), a herb, the seeds of which are moderately warming, pungent, and aromatic, formerly used as a soothing medicine for children; also known as dillseed.</li>
<li>A cucumber pickled with <a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a> flavoring
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a> pickle</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a fool.
<ul><li><b>2016</b>, Robert G. Barrett, <i>And <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Fun Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> Done: A <a href = vnd.unilang:les.html>Les</a> Norton Novel</i>
<dl><dd>He could go <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a> his way among the poms, but he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> that drunk he'd probably only make a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a></b> of himself</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">herb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">anet</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">dillseed</span>, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Peucedanum_graveolens" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Peucedanum graveolens"><i>Peucedanum graveolens</i></a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">type of pickle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a> pickle</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">dills</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">dilling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">dilled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To cook or flavor with <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a></a>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  Anatoly (<a href = vnd.unilang:tony.html>Tony</a>) Kandiew,  <cite>Red <a href = vnd.unilang:devils.html>Devils</a></cite>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 139:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">My mother would pickle them and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a></b> them, and <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> still <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> an abundance of fresh vegetables left.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dull</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">dills</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">dilling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">dilled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To still; to assuage; to calm; to soothe, as one in pain.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1775</b>,  Robert Baillie,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>Letters</a> and Journals: Written by the deceased <a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. Robert Baillie, Principal of the University of Glasgow</cite>, page 252:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The noise of the Queen's voyage to France <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>dilled</b> down ; no money  for her furniture will be got in haste; and the Cardinal <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> no will of her mother.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1829</b>,  <cite>Publications <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Issue 25, Volume 2</cite>, page x:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The innocent <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> punished. The gear <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> payed and the <a href = vnd.unilang:thieves.html>thieves</a> <b>dilled</b> down.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1829</b>,  John Spalding amp; James Skene,  <cite>The History of the <a href = vnd.unilang:troubles.html>Troubles</a> and Memorable Transactions in Scotland</cite>, page vii:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The Provincial Assembly sits down. <a href = vnd.unilang:dr.html>Dr</a>. Guild moderator. <a href = vnd.unilang:dr.html>Dr</a>. Scroggie preaches. His sermon found faulty. It <b>dills</b> down.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1890</b>,  Thomas Nield,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a> Cromwell, Lord Protector of England: A Drama</cite>, page 23:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> nought to call them back, while these Curmudgeon generals <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a></b> down in their fear.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1938</b>,  Alexander Ross,  <cite>Scot. Text S</cite>, page 195:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">That now the dinn <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>' it wad soon <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dill.html>dill</a></b> down, An' but a story at the last be found.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***dimmer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dimmer.html>dimmer</a> (107618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dim</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/dimmer" class="extiw" title="w:dimmer"><a href = vnd.unilang:dimmer.html>dimmer</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/dimmer" class="extiw" title="w:dimmer">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dimmer.html>dimmer</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dimmers.html>dimmers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A rheostat that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used to vary the intensity of a domestic electric light</li>
<li>A switch used to select between the low and high headlamp beam on a road vehicle. (usually as "<a href = vnd.unilang:dimmer.html>dimmer</a> switch", primarily in North America; elsewhere "dipswitch" or "dipper switch")</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">dipswitch</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">dipper</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dingen.html>dingen</a> (229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dingen.html>dingen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to convene, to plead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thingon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þingōną</i>. The verb <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> originally weak, but became strong by analogy with other verbs.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dingen.html>dingen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to solicit</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ding.html>ding</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">dinken</i>, a regional variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:denken.html>denken</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:dink.html>dink</a></strong> (<i>present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af pres-form-of" lang="af"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:dink.html>dink</a></strong></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:denkende.html>denkende</a></b>, <i>past</i> <b class="Latn" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="af">dog</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af past | ptcp-form-of" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedag.html>gedag</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af past | ptcp-form-of" lang="af">gedog</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af past | ptcp-form-of" lang="af">gedink</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to think
<ul><li><b>1939</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:jaarboek.html>Jaarboek</a></i>, page 44:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>Ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gedag.html>gedag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:behoefte.html>behoefte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pleit.html>pleit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> 'n dergelike samewerikng <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1951</b>, <i>Suid-Afrikaanse Hofverslae</i>, volume 3, page 79:
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href = vnd.unilang:ek.html>ek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gedag.html>gedag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> my <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> se <a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>dood</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sal.html>sal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geraak.html>geraak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1993</b>, <i>A Grammar of <a href = vnd.unilang:afrikaans.html>Afrikaans</a></i>, Bruce Donaldson, page 223:
<dl><dd>Hy <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gedag.html>gedag</a></b>/gedog/gedink <a href = vnd.unilang:ek.html>ek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sou.html>sou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eers.html>eers</a> môre <a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>kom</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The regular past form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> gedink</i> can be used in all senses.</li>
<li>The irregular past forms <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a>, dog; <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedag.html>gedag</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> gedog</i> can only be used in the sense of “to believe, to reckon (that)”, but not in the sense of “to think about, to ponder”.</li></ul>
</body>

***dino.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dino.html>dino</a> (14156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dino.html>dino</a></i>. Equivalent to a clipping of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dinosaurus.html>dinosaurus</a></i>. The term became especially prominent after the release of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jurassic_Park" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jurassic Park">Jurassic Park</a> in 1993, but predated the <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a> by at least one or two years.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dino.html>dino</a></span>, a dinosaur; archosaur of the super-order Dinosauria. <span class="defdate">[from late 20th c.]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dino.html>dino</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dinsdag.html>dinsdag</a> (2606)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dinxdach</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dinxendag</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dinsendach</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ding.html>ding</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing, assembly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <ol><li>Tuesday</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*deuʀ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*deuzą</i>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">dēor</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">dýr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="osx"><a href = vnd.unilang:dior.html>dior</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>animal</li></ol>

***diplomaat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:diplomaat.html>diplomaat</a> (11688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">diplomate</i>, a derivation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dīplōmaticus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diplomaat.html>diplomaat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diplomaten.html>diplomaten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diplomaat.html>diplomaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A diplomat, accredited in diplomacy.</li>
<li>A diplomatic person, who <a href = vnd.unilang:shows.html>shows</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tact.html>tact</a> and insight.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diploma.html>diploma</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diplomatie.html>diplomatie</a></span></li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dīrigēns</i>, present participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dīrigō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I direct</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. </p>

</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">diriger</i>.

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to direct, to lead</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <span class="Latn" lang="en">conduct</span>, to musically direct an orchestra, choir or other ensemble</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <span class="Latn" lang="en">address</span>, to send (to)</li>
